```bash

Using 16bit Automatic Mixed Precision (AMP)
```

# 10.语义门控过滤车辆行人背景树木

训练配置如下：

```bash
aggregator:
  class: MixVPR
  module: src.models.aggregators
  params:
    in_channels: 1024
    in_h: 20
    in_w: 20
    mix_depth: 4
    mlp_ratio: 1
    out_channels: 512
    out_rows: 4
backbone:
  class: ResNet
  module: src.models.backbones
  params:
    backbone_name: resnet50
    crop_last_block: true
    num_unfrozen_blocks: 1
    pretrained: true
compile: false
datamodule:
  batch_size: 100
  cities: all
  img_per_place: 4
  num_workers: 8
  train_image_size:
  - 320
  - 320
  train_set_name: gsv-cities
  val_image_size: null
  val_set_names:
  - msls-val
  - pitts30k-val
dev: false
display_theme: default
distillation:
  distill_warmup_steps: 1500
  dynamic_categories:
  - car
  - truck
  - bus
  - person
  - pedestrian
  - bicycle
  - motorcycle
  - tree
  - vegetation
  - sky
  - cloud
  enabled: true
  lambda_global: 0.1
  lambda_region: 0.05
  mode: region_semantic_gate
  proj_dim: null
  tau: 0.07
  teacher:
    model_name: ViT-B-16
    pretrained: openai
loss_function:
  class: VPRLossFunction
  module: src.losses
  params:
    loss_fn_name: MultiSimilarityLoss
    miner_name: MultiSimilarityMiner
seed: 42
silent: false
train: true
trainer:
  lr: 0.0002
  lr_mult: 0.1
  max_epochs: 40
  milestones:
  - 10
  - 20
  - 30
  optimizer: adamw
  warmup: 1500
  wd: 0.001

```

# 11. 语义门控仅过滤车辆行人

训练配置如下：

```bash
aggregator:
  class: MixVPR
  module: src.models.aggregators
  params:
    in_channels: 1024
    in_h: 20
    in_w: 20
    mix_depth: 4
    mlp_ratio: 1
    out_channels: 512
    out_rows: 4
backbone:
  class: ResNet
  module: src.models.backbones
  params:
    backbone_name: resnet50
    crop_last_block: true
    num_unfrozen_blocks: 1
    pretrained: true
compile: false
datamodule:
  batch_size: 100
  cities: all
  img_per_place: 4
  num_workers: 8
  train_image_size:
  - 320
  - 320
  train_set_name: gsv-cities
  val_image_size: null
  val_set_names:
  - msls-val
  - pitts30k-val
dev: false
display_theme: default
distillation:
  distill_warmup_steps: 1500
  dynamic_categories:
  - car
  - truck
  - bus
  - person
  - pedestrian
  - bicycle
  - motorcycle
  - tree
  - vegetation
  - sky
  - cloud
  enabled: true
  lambda_global: 0.1
  lambda_region: 0.05
  mode: region_semantic_gate
  proj_dim: null
  tau: 0.07
  teacher:
    model_name: ViT-B-16
    pretrained: openai
loss_function:
  class: VPRLossFunction
  module: src.losses
  params:
    loss_fn_name: MultiSimilarityLoss
    miner_name: MultiSimilarityMiner
seed: 42
silent: false
train: true
trainer:
  lr: 0.0002
  lr_mult: 0.1
  max_epochs: 40
  milestones:
  - 10
  - 20
  - 30
  optimizer: adamw
  warmup: 1500
  wd: 0.001

```

最好的三次结果如下；

```bash
epoch(23)_step(15024)_R1[0.8649]_R5[0.9297]
epoch(25)_step(16276)_R1[0.8662]_R5[0.9297]
epoch(27)_step(17528)_R1[0.8662]_R5[0.9297]
```
